Now I can see the implementation. Let me focus on the `incdec_number` and `_get_incdec_value` functions (lines 532-605).\n\nLet me analyze the bugs:\n\n1. **Encoded sequences corruption**: Looking at line 598:\n```python\nmatch = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter())\n```\n\nThis regex matches:\n- `(.*\\D|^)` - Either anything ending with a non-digit, or the start\n- `(0*)` - Zero or more leading zeros\n- `(\\d+)` - One or more digits\n- `(.*)` - Everything after\n\nThe issue is that when `getter()` is called on certain URL segments (like `host`, `path`, `query`), these are NOT url-encoded. The `getter()` functions return decoded versions. So if I have a URL with `%3A` (encoded colon), when we call `url.host()` or `url.path()`, the `%` and the digits in `3A` are treated as part of the number matching.\n\nFor example, if the URL is `http://localhost/%3A5`:\n- `url.path()` returns `/%3A5`\n- The regex will match: pre=`/%`, zeroes=``, number=`3`, post=`A5`\n- If we increment by 1, we get `4` instead of `3`, resulting in `/%4A5`\n- This corrupts the `%3A` sequence!\n\n2. **Negative values allowed**: Looking at line 537-540:\n```python\nif incdec == 'decrement':\n    if val <= 0:\n        raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {}!\".format(val), url)\n    val -= count\n```\n\nThe check is `if val <= 0`, which means we raise an error if the value is already 0 or negative. \n\nThe problem is we don't validate that `val - count` stays non-negative. If I have `page_1` and decrement by 2, the initial check passes since val=1 > 0, but then `val -= count` produces `val = -1`, which gets written back to the URL.\n\n3. **URL-encoded data is lost**: When we call `url.host()`, `url.path()`, etc., Qt returns decoded versions. If the original URL was `http://example.com/page%20test`, calling `url.path()` returns `/page test` (decoded). But actually, `%C3%B6` is the URL encoding for `ö`. The test name is \"test_no_number\", so it seems the current behavior is to treat the encoded data as if it could contain numbers.\n\nNow I understand the bugs:\n\n1. **Encoded sequences corruption**: When we have a URL like `http://localhost/%3A5`, the path is `/%3A5`. When we call `url.path()`, it returns `/%3A5` (not decoded at that level, it's still encoded). The regex `r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)'` matches:\n   - `(.*\\D|^)` = `/%` (ends with %)\n   - `(0*)` = `` (no zeros)\n   - `(\\d+)` = `3` (matches the digit after %)\n   - `(.*)` = `A5`\n   \n   So if we increment by 1, we get `/%4A5` instead of `/%3A6`.\n\n2. **Negative values**: Looking at the existing test `test_number_below_0` on line 735-739:\n   ```python\n   def test_number_below_0(self):\n       \"\"\"Test incdec_number with a number <0 after decrementing.\"\"\"\n       with pytest.raises(urlutils.IncDecError):\n           urlutils.incdec_number(QUrl('http://example.com/page_0.html'),\n                                  'decrement')\n   ```\n   The current code checks if the initial value is <= 0, but it doesn't check if `val - count` would go negative. For example, if we have `page_1.html` and decrement by 2, the initial check passes (1 > 0), but then `val -= 2` gives us `-1`.\n\n3. **URL-encoded data loss**: Different encoding strategies need {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_017vRYqdVBZ7DvtHFijG69KN","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Right, there are circular import issues with the full qutebrowser setup. Let me extract just the code I need to test and create a self-contained test file. First, let me understand better by reading the code and analyzing what the bugs are.\n\nLooking at the `incdec_number` function again:\n\n```python\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \"\"\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\"\"\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    # This should always succeed because we match \\d+\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val <= 0:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {}!\".format(val), url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for indec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n```\n\nThe bugs are:\n\n1. **Negative value bug**: The check is `if val <= 0`, which checks if the CURRENT value is <= 0. It doesn't check if `val - count` would be negative. For example:\n   - URL: `http://example.com/page_1`\n   - Decrement by 2\n   - Current val = 1\n   - Check: 1 > 0, so it passes\n   - After decrement: val = 1 - 2 = -1\n   - This should raise an error, but it doesn't!\n\n2. **Encoded sequence corruption**: When dealing with URLs that have encoded sequences with digits:\n   - URL: `http://localhost/%3A5` \n   - path() returns `/:5` (decoded)\n   - The regex matches and finds `5` as the number\n   - When we increment, we get `/:6`\n   - When we set it back with `url.setPath(\"/:6\")`, Qt encodes it back to `/%3A6`\n   \n   This seems to work correctly actually. Let me reconsider what the actual issue is by checking the problem statement more carefully.\n\nThe bug report states that percent-encoded characters containing digits (like `%3A` for colon) get corrupted during increment operations. The `5` should be the only part that changes, not the `3` in `%3A`. When I call `url.path()` on `http://localhost/%3A5`, Qt decodes it to `/:5`, so the colon is already decoded. The regex then matches just the `5` at the end, which should be correct behavior.\n\nIncrementing to `/:6` and setting it back should re-encode to `/%3A6`. But the bug report suggests something like `/%4A5` appears instead. This makes me wonder if the issue occurs when using `url.path(QUrl.FullyEncoded)` rather than the default decoding behavior.\n\nLooking at how `incdec_number` actually works—it retrieves the path via `url.path()` (which returns decoded), performs regex matching on that decoded string, increments the number, then passes the result back through `url.setPath()`. The function treats both getter and setter as callable objects, so the flow is: decode → match → increment → re-encode. This should theoretically work correctly, but there might be an edge case in how the setter handles the modified path. Unless the issue manifests differently depending on URL structure. Let me examine what each segment getter returns—particularly for query and anchor, where I'm uncertain whether `url.query()` and `url.fragment()` return encoded or decoded Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # Order as they appear in a URL\n    segment_modifiers = [\n        ('host', url.host, url.setHost),\n        ('port', lambda: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n         lambda x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n        ('path', url.path, url.setPath),\n        ('query', url.query, url.setQuery),\n        ('anchor', url.fragment, url.setFragment),\n    ]\n    # Encoded sequences in query/fragment are corrupted when modified\n2. Negative values are allowed when they shouldn't be\n3. URL-encoded data inconsistency across different URL segments\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# Copy of the functions under test (to avoid circular imports)\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass IncDecError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, msg, url):\n        super().__init__(msg)\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = msg\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())\n\n\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \"\"\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\"\"\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val <= 0:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {}!\".format(val), url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for indec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid URL\")\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # Order as they appear in a URL\n    segment_modifiers = [\n        ('host', url.host, url.setHost),\n        ('port', lambda: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n         lambda x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n        ('path', url.path, url.setPath),\n        ('query', url.query, url.setQuery),\n        ('anchor', url.fragment, url.setFragment),\n    ]\n    # We're searching the last number so we walk the url segments backwards\n    for segment, getter, setter in reversed(segment_modifiers):\n        if segment not in segments:\n            continue\n\n        # Get the last number in a string\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', getter())\n        if not match:\n            continue\n\n        setter(_get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count))\n        return url\n\n    raise IncDecError(\"No number found in URL!\", url)\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# Regression Tests\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass TestEncodedSequenceCorruption:\n    \"\"\"Test that encoded sequences in URLs are not corrupted during increment/decrement.\"\"\"\n\n    def test_number_followed_by_encoded_colon(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that a number followed by %3A is handled correctly.\n\n        BUG: When we have 5%3A in the query, the regex matches the '3' in '%3A'\n        (the LAST digit) rather than the '5', because the regex looks for the\n        LAST number in the string.\n\n        URL: http://example.com/?page=5%3A\n        When incrementing, the buggy code matches '3' and makes it '4',\n        resulting in: http://example.com/?page=5%4A (CORRUPTED!)\n\n        Expected: http://example.com/?page=6%3A (increment the 5, preserve %3A)\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/?page=5%3A\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'query'})\n\n        # After incrementing, we should have page=6%3A, not page=5%4A\n        query = result.query()\n        assert \"page=6%3A\" in query, \\\n            f\"Expected page=6%3A, but got: {query}\"\n        assert \"page=5%4A\" not in query, \\\n            f\"Query has corrupted encoding (5%4A): {query}\"\n\n    def test_number_followed_by_encoded_digit_sequence(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that number before %35 (encoded 5) is handled correctly.\n\n        BUG: If we have page=9%35, the regex finds '3' as the last digit\n        and increments it to '4', corrupting the encoding.\n\n        Expected: increment the 9 to 10\n        Actual (buggy): increment the 3 in %35 to 4, resulting in %45\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/?page=9%35\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'query'})\n\n        query = result.query()\n        # Should have either page=10%35 or similar, not corrupted %45\n        assert \"%35\" in query or \"5\" in query, \\\n            f\"Encoding or number lost in query: {query}\"\n        assert \"%45\" not in query and \"%4\" not in query, \\\n            f\"Query encoding corrupted (has %4x): {query}\"\n\n    def test_fragment_with_number_before_encoding(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that fragment with number followed by encoding is handled correctly.\n\n        Similar to query corruption bug but in fragment.\n        \"\"\"\n        url = QUrl(\"http://example.com/#section-3%3Aend\")\n        result = incdec_number(url, 'increment', segments={'anchor'})\n\n        fragment = result.fragment()\n        # Simulate what happens with the regex on encoded query values\n        query = \"key=%3A5\"  # This is what url.query() returns\n        match = re.fullmatch(r'(.*\\D|^)(0*)(\\d+)(.*)', query)\n\n        assert match is not None, \"Regex should match\"\n        pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n\n        # The bug: regex matches '3' as the number, not '5'\n        assert number == '3', f\"BUG DEMO: Regex matched {number}, should be 5\"\n        assert post == 'A5', f\"BUG DEMO: Post should be 'A5', got {post}\"\n\n        # Current check\n        if val <= 0:\n            would_raise = True\n        else:\n            would_raise = False\n\n        # BUG: Check passes because val=1 > 0\n        assert not would_raise, \"BUG DEMO: Check incorrectly passes for val=1\"\n\n        # Encoded sequences in query/fragment are corrupted when modified\n2. Negative values are allowed when they shouldn't be\n3. URL-encoded data inconsistency across different URL segments\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nimport pytest\nfrom PyQt5.QtCore import QUrl\n\n\n# ============================================================================\n# Copy of the functions under test (to avoid circular imports)\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass IncDecError(Exception):\n    \"\"\"Exception raised by incdec_number on problems.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, msg, url):\n        super().__init__(msg)\n        self.url = url\n        self.msg = msg\n\n    def __str__(self):\n        return '{}: {}'.format(self.msg, self.url.toString())\n\n\ndef _get_incdec_value(match, incdec, url, count):\n    \"\"\"Get an incremented/decremented URL based on a URL match.\"\"\"\n    pre, zeroes, number, post = match.groups()\n    val = int(number)\n    if incdec == 'decrement':\n        if val <= 0:\n            raise IncDecError(\"Can't decrement {}!\".format(val), url)\n        val -= count\n    elif incdec == 'increment':\n        val += count\n    else:\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid value {} for indec!\".format(incdec))\n    if zeroes:\n        if len(number) < len(str(val)):\n            zeroes = zeroes[1:]\n        elif len(number) > len(str(val)):\n            zeroes += '0'\n    return ''.join([pre, zeroes, str(val), post])\n\n\ndef incdec_number(url, incdec, count=1, segments=None):\n    \"\"\"Find a number in the url and increment or decrement it.\"\"\"\n    if not url.isValid():\n        raise ValueError(\"Invalid URL\")\n\n    if segments is None:\n        segments = {'path', 'query'}\n    valid_segments = {'host', 'port', 'path', 'query', 'anchor'}\n    if segments - valid_segments:\n        extra_elements = segments - valid_segments\n        raise IncDecError(\"Invalid segments: {}\".format(\n            ', '.join(extra_elements)), url)\n\n    # Make a copy of the QUrl so we don't modify the original\n    url = QUrl(url)\n    # Order as they appear in a URL\n    segment_modifiers = [\n        ('host', url.host, url.setHost),\n        ('port', lambda: str(url.port()) if url.port() > 0 else '',\n         lambda x: url.setPort(int(x))),\n        ('path', url.path, url.setPath),\n        ('query', url.query, url.setQuery),\n        ('anchor', url.fragment, url.setFragment),\n    ]\n    #
